<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonsondergang.html>zonsondergang</a> (4307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sonne-onderganc</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergang.html>ondergang</a></i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sout</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:salt.html>salt</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>noun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saltą</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>adjective</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saltaz</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*séh₂l-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*séh₂ls</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Salz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sâlt</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:salt.html>salt</a></i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:salt.html>salt</a></i>.
